
####################################################################################################
#
# Disassembly listing of binary '7DBC' (8061, 1 bank) by SAD Version 4.0.5 (25/02/2020)
# See '7DBC_msg.txt' for warnings, results and other information

# Explanation of extra flags and formats - 
#   R general register. Extra prefix letters shown for mixed size opcodes (e.g DIVW)
#   l=long (4 bytes), w=word (2 bytes), y=byte, s=signed. Unsigned is default.
#   [ ]=use value as an address   (addresses are always word) 
#   @=value is an address (to symbol),  '++' increment register after operation.
# Processor status flags (for conditional jumps)
#   CY=carry, STC=sticky, OVF=overflow, OVT=overflow trap
#
####################################################################################################


################################################################################
# 0000-00FF 8061 Internal Registers (256 Bytes)
################################################################################

#ADDR	Size	Read				Size	Write
#-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
#0000	B/W	Zero
#0001	B/W	Zero
#0002	B	LSO port (Non-bidirectional)	B	LSO port (Non-bidirectional)
#0003	B	Bidirectional I/O port			B	Bidirectional I/O port
#0004	B	A/D Result Lo					B	A/D command (Channel #)
#0005	B	A/D Result Hi					B	Watchdog timer
#0006	W	Master I/O timer 
#0008	B	Interrupt mask					B	Interrupt mask
#0009	B	Interrupt pending				B	Interrupt pending
#000A	B	I/O status						B	I/O status
#000B	B	HSI sample register
#000C	B	HSI data mask					B	HSI data mask
#000D	B	HSI data hold					B	HSO command hold
#000E	W	HSI time hold					W	HSO time hold
#0010	B/W	Stack Pointer Lo byte			B/W	Stack Pointer Lo byte
#0011	B/W	Stack Pointer Hi byte			B/W	Stack Pointer Hi byte
#0012	B/W General purpose registers		B/W General purpose registers
#00FF	B/W General purpose registers		B/W General purpose registers

################################################################################
# 2000-2003 reset entry point
################################################################################
2000: ff                  nop                    
2001: fa                  di                     disable intps;
2002: 21,9a               sjmp  219e             goto init;

################################################################################


2004: 00,00               word      0            FIXSUM                            #usually zero
2006: ff,df               word   dfff                                              #unknown; same value as A9L
2008: 00,ff               word   ff00                                              #unknown; same value as A9L
200a: 46,eb               word   eb46            ROM_TO                            #checksum?
200c: 00,a0               word   a000            SMP_Base_Address                  #same value as A9L
200e: 5d,00               word     5d            CC_EXECUTION_TIME                 #calibration console, same value as A9L

################################################################################
# 2010-201F Interrupt Vectors
################################################################################

2010: f0,27               vect  27f0             I_HSO_2
2012: dc,27               vect  27dc             I_Timer_OVF
2014: ef,27               vect  27ef             I_Ignore
2016: ef,27               vect  27ef             I_Ignore
2018: ef,27               vect  27ef             I_Ignore
201a: 5d,26               vect  265d             I_HSO_1
201c: ef,27               vect  27ef             I_Ignore
201e: c9,27               vect  27c9             I_HSI_0

################################################################################

2020: 08                  byte      8            NUM_OF_LEVELS
2021: 01                  byte      1            NUM_OF_CALIBRATIONS

################################################################################

################################################################################

2022: 50,6f               word   6f50            RF0
2024: 22,72               word   7222            RF2
2026: 24,75               word   7524            RF4
2028: b4,76               word   76b4            RF6
202a: 76,79               word   7976            RF8

2032 -> 20a1 = 0xff  ## Ignored ## 


################################################################################
# Reset:
# 1: clear memory from 0012 - 02A0, SP is temporarily used, ends up back at 02A2 when done
#    note that we did not clear 02A2 which holds our return address (top of stack)
# 2: load initial memory state from ROM

#R2A - is VIP_mode_flag (Vehicle Interface Port / DLC control)
################################################################################

   setup_initial_state:
20a2: fa                  di                     disable intps;                    #disable interupts, (they were already disabled, seems redundant?)
20a3: ff                  nop                    
20a4: 11,0c               clrb  Rc               HSI_Mask = 0;                     #all HSI inputs disabled
20a6: a1,12,00,10         ldw   R10,12           StackPtr = 12;                    #temporarily point the SP at 0012; we are going to use it to clear memory
20aa: c6,11,00            stb   R0,[R10++]       [StackPtr] = 0;                   #clear current memory location and increment SP
20ad: 17,05               incb  R5               WDG_Timer++;                      #inc WD timer
20af: 3e,2a,03            jb    B6,R2a,20b5      if (B6_VIP_mode_flag = 1) goto 20b5;   #if VIP_mode_flag (NO_START_TESTS) is set (KOEO)
20b2: 35,2a,08            jnb   B5,R2a,20bd      if (B5_VIP_mode_flag = 1)  {      #and/or if VIP_mode_flag (RUNNING_TESTS) is set (KOER)
20b5: 89,2a,00,10         cmpw  R10,2a                                             #and sp points at = R2A (VIP_mode_flag)
20b9: d7,02               jne   20bd             if (StackPtr = 2a)  {             #
20bb: 17,10               incb  R10              StackPtr++; } }                   #inc SP and skip clearing VIP_mode_flag
20bd: 17,05               incb  R5               WDG_Timer++;                      #inc WD timer
20bf: 89,a0,02,10         cmpw  R10,2a0          
20c3: d3,e5               jnc   20aa             if (StackPtr < 2a0) goto 20aa;    #if SP less than 02A0, not finished clearing memory, else done
#-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
20c5: a1,62,6a,14         ldw   R14,6a62         R14 = 6a62;                       #R14 points to first init table in rom
20c9: 89,ff,ff,14         cmpw  R14,ffff                                           #if R14 points to FFFF (no more table to process, break)
20cd: df,20               je    20ef             if (R14 = ffff) goto 20ef;        #
20cf: a2,15,1a            ldw   R1a,[R14++]      R1a = [R14++];                    #R1A is RAM offset high byte (0000), low byte is overwritten
20d2: a2,15,16            ldw   R16,[R14++]      R16 = [R14++];                    #R16 is pointer to last entry in table (contains address of next table)
20d5: 88,16,14            cmpw  R14,R16                                            #
20d8: db,0e               jc    20e8             if (R14 >= R16) goto 20e8;        #while we are not passed the end of table
20da: b2,15,1a            ldb   R1a,[R14++]      R1a = [R14++];                    #pointer to next byte in list
20dd: b2,1a,1c            ldb   R1c,[R1a]        R1c = [R1a];                      #store the bytes value into R1C, this value will be RAM location low byte
20e0: 92,15,1c            orb   R1c,[R14++]      R1c |= [R14++];                   #the next byte is the data, or it with current value (but we've just cleared mem so should have n
                                                                                   o effect?)
20e3: c6,1a,1c            stb   R1c,[R1a]        [R1a] = R1c;                      #store the value (2nd byte) into the register (1st byte)
20e6: 27,ed               sjmp  20d5             goto 20d5;                        #contine until end of list

20e8: d9,b8               jgtu  20a2             if (R1c > 0) goto setup_initial_state;   #R1C should never be larger than R14, oops.
20ea: a2,16,14            ldw   R14,[R16]        R14 = [R16];                      #R14 now points at next table in ROM
20ed: 27,da               sjmp  20c9             goto 20c9;                        #continue til we've processed all init tables
#-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

20ef: 3d,2a,06            jb    B5,R2a,20f8      if (B5_VIP_mode_flag = 0)  {
20f2: 3e,2a,03            jb    B6,R2a,20f8      if (B6_VIP_mode_flag = 0)  {
20f5: 91,01,a2            orb   Ra2,1            B0_Ra2 = 1; } }
20f8: a3,01,00,0d,14      ldw   R14,[R0+d00]     R14 = CC_PRESENT;
20fd: 99,2a,15            cmpb  R15,2a           
2100: d7,0e               jne   2110             if (R15 != 2a) goto 2110;
2102: a3,01,80,0c,14      ldw   R14,[R0+c80]     R14 = [c80];
2107: 36,14,06            jnb   B6,R14,2110      if (B6_R14 = 0) goto 2110;
210a: a1,00,c2,14         ldw   R14,c200         R14 = c200;
210e: 20,30               sjmp  2140             goto 2140;

2110: af,01,30,09,16      ldzbw R16,[R0+930]     wR16 = [930];
2115: 51,02,16,18         an3b  R18,R16,2        R18 = R16 & 2;
2119: 71,18,16            an2b  R16,18           R16 &= 18;
211c: 18,01,18            shrb  R18,1            R18 >>= 1;                        #[ R18 /= 2] 
211f: 18,02,16            shrb  R16,2            R16 >>= 2;                        #[ R16 /= 4] 
2122: 90,18,16            orb   R16,R18          R16 |= R18;
2125: b3,01,21,20,18      ldb   R18,[R0+2021]    R18 = NUM_OF_CALIBRATIONS;
212a: 15,18               decb  R18              R18--;
212c: 98,16,18            cmpb  R18,R16          
212f: db,02               jc    2133             if (R18 < R16)  {
2131: 01,16               clrw  R16              R16 = 0; }
2133: 5f,01,20,20,16,14   ml3b  R14,R16,[R0+2020] wR14 = R16 * NUM_OF_LEVELS;
2139: 65,11,10,14         ad2w  R14,1011         R14 += 1011;
213d: 09,01,14            shlw  R14,1            R14 <<= 1;                        #[ R14 *= 2] 
2140: a1,f0,00,18         ldw   R18,f0           R18 = f0;
2144: b3,01,20,20,1a      ldb   R1a,[R0+2020]    R1a = NUM_OF_LEVELS;
2149: a2,15,1c            ldw   R1c,[R14++]      R1c = [R14++];
214c: c2,19,1c            stw   R1c,[R18++]      [R18++] = R1c;
214f: e0,1a,f7            djnz  R1a,2149         R1a--;
                                                 if (R1a != 0) goto 2149;
2152: a3,01,3c,03,30      ldw   R30,[R0+33c]     R30 = [33c];
2157: 8b,f3,7e,02,30      cmpw  R30,[Rf2+27e]    
215c: d1,07               jleu  2165             if (R30 <= [74a0]) goto 2165;
215e: 8b,f3,80,02,30      cmpw  R30,[Rf2+280]    
2163: d3,09               jnc   216e             if (R30 >= [74a2])  {
2165: a1,80,a2,30         ldw   R30,a280         R30 = a280;
2169: c3,01,3c,03,30      stw   R30,[R0+33c]     [33c] = R30; }
216e: c7,01,de,01,b4      stb   Rb4,[R0+1de]     [1de] = Rb4;
2173: ef,90,49            call  6b06             common_Sub22();
2176: 11,09               clrb  R9               INT_Pend = 0;
2178: 32,0a,06            jnb   B2,Ra,2181       if (HSI_Ready = 1)  {
217b: b0,0d,00            ldb   R0,Rd            R0 = HSI_Data;
217e: ff                  nop                    
217f: 27,f7               sjmp  2178             goto 2178; }

2181: b0,0b,8e            ldb   R8e,Rb           R8e = HSI_Sample;
2184: b1,a1,08            ldb   R8,a1            INT_Mask = a1;
2187: b1,a7,0c            ldb   Rc,a7            HSI_Mask = a7;
218a: 9b,f7,c1,02,00      cmpb  R0,[Rf6+2c1]     
218f: d7,03               jne   2194             if ([7975] = 0)  {
2191: b1,a5,0c            ldb   Rc,a5            HSI_Mask = a5; }
2194: 45,03,00,06,0e      ad3w  Re,R6,3          HSI_Time = IO_Timer + 3;
2199: b1,2a,0d            ldb   Rd,2a            HSO_Cmd = 2a;
219c: fb                  ei                     enable intps;
219d: f0                  ret                    return;

################################################################################
#Init: we jump here from 2000 after disabling interrupts
#R2A - is VIP_mode_flag (Vehicle Interface Port / DLC control)
################################################################################

   init:
219e: 11,2a               clrb  R2a              VIP_mode_flag = 0;                #clear the VIP_mode_flag; all bits
21a0: a1,a2,02,10         ldw   R10,2a2          StackPtr = 2a2;                   #initialise stack pointer at 02A2, stack grows downwards
21a4: 2e,fc               scall 20a2             setup_initial_state();            #save return address to stack; interrupts enabled before returning

################################################################################
#EEC_main_loop: cycles through routines, should never terminate
#R94 - is current routine offset, will be 0 first time through
#R72 - is current RAM address pointer
#R30 - is the calculated next routine address
################################################################################
   EEC_main_loop:
21a6: 99,7c,94            cmpb  R94,7c                                             #loop sanity check
21a9: db,14               jc    21bf             if (R94 < 7c)  {                  #21D6 + offset 7C equals 2252; we are out of array bounds, goto HANG
21ab: ac,94,30            ldzbw R30,R94          wR30 = yR94;                      #R30 = copy of current routine offset
21ae: 65,d6,21,30         ad2w  R30,21d6         R30 += 21d6;                      #R30 = array start address + current routine offset
21b2: c9,a6,21            push  21a6             push(EEC_main_loop);              #save EEC_main_loop address to stack
21b5: ca,30               push  [R30]            push([R30]);                      #save calculated subroutine address to stack
21b7: a1,80,01,72         ldw   R72,180          R72 = 180;                        #re-init RAM pointer(s) after every function call
21bb: 75,02,94            ad2b  R94,2            R94 += 2;                         #increment to next routine offset address (ready for next loop)
21be: f0                  ret                    return; }                         #jump to calculated subroutine address

   WATCHDOG_HANG:
21bf: 27,fe               sjmp  21bf             goto WATCHDOG_HANG;               #infinite loop for watchdog (we crashed!)

################################################################################
#main_loop_selection: update run-mode loop selection and restart from beginning
#possible run modes are NORMAL NO_START_TESTS(KOEO) RUNNING_TESTS(KOER)
#R2A - is VIP_mode_flag (Vehicle Interface Port / DLC control)
#R94 - is current routine offset
################################################################################

   main_loop_selection:
21c1: 3e,2a,03            jb    B6,R2a,21c7      if (B6_VIP_mode_flag = 1) goto 21c7;   #if VIP_mode_flag (NO_START_TESTS) is set (KOEO); else break
21c4: 31,2a,04            jnb   B1,R2a,21cb      if (B1_VIP_mode_flag = 1)  {      #if VIP_mode_flag (VEHICLE_SPEED_CONTROL_TESTS) (cruise) not set; break
21c7: b1,3c,94            ldb   R94,3c           R94 = 3c;                         #set routine to loop B (2212; on-demand KOEO self tests)
21ca: f0                  ret                    return; }                         #return to EEC_main_loop

21cb: 35,2a,04            jnb   B5,R2a,21d2      if (B5_VIP_mode_flag = 1)  {      #if VIP_mode_flag (RUNNING_TESTS) not set (KOER); break
21ce: b1,58,94            ldb   R94,58           R94 = 58;                         #set routine to loop C (222E; on-demand KOER self tests)
21d1: f0                  ret                    return; }                         #return to EEC_main_loop

21d2: b1,00,94            ldb   R94,0            R94 = 0;                          #set routine to loop A (21D6; normal operation)
21d5: f0                  ret                    return;                           #return to EEC_main_loop
